info:1 Review
rating:4.7
posted:Posted April 29, 2024
msg:I chose this hotel based on my own hotel experience. The hotel is very good, with plenty of seats in the lobby and a very thoughtful layout. I especially like the bookshelves used as partition screens in the lobby. The hotel is located in the pedestrian street of Zhongji's own business center, which is very convenient to enter and exit. It takes 5 to 15 minutes to walk to Yiyuan, the south gate of Slender West Lake, Vientiane (a large commercial center), and 7-11. There is also a restaurant 20 meters away from the hotel entrance that is open until 5 am. The room is of a suitable size. The entrance is the porch, and the main body of the room is a right-angle turn. The privacy protection is very good (the right side of Figure 1 is the corridor connecting the porch to the room). The breakfast variety is rich enough, and the quality of the dishes is also good. Adults eat comfortably and children eat at ease. Originally, we were going to pay for breakfast for the children separately (58 yuan for adult breakfast, 29 yuan for children under 12 years old at half price). When we registered the bill with the room number at the entrance of the restaurant, a children's breakfast was given on the spot. Manager Cai of the restaurant is very enthusiastic, cheerful, and friendly. What needs to be reminded is that the room's hygienic corners (for example, screen windows and wardrobe hanging rods) should be dusted regularly.
